[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m` file[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. While processing entries, the Jazzer [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal` sanitizer flagged an entry path that would escape the intended [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction directory, throwing:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal: [0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-[0m[39m*[0m[35m/output/[0m[39m…[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This indicates that a path from the archive was used directly without sufficient [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitization, allowing an attacker-controlled archive to write files outside the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget folder.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The sanitizer labels this as a “File path traversal” vulnerability, where [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted archive entry names can traverse parent directories or target arbitrary [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfilesystem locations.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important Observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash originates in [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.checkPath`, hooked by [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer on file I/O calls.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace shows the path hook triggered inside `TikaUntar.main` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m47[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring archive expansion.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Instrumentation logs indicate extensive coverage of Apache Commons Compress and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache Commons IO classes, including `TarArchiveInputStream`, `ArchiveUtils`, and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvarious IO utilities—key areas for file extraction logic.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A reproducer Java file [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Crash_*.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was generated for deterministic [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdebugging.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **Tika CLI Extraction Logic**  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `org.apache.tika.cli.TikaUntar` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparticularly around line [0m[1;36m47[0m[39m where [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction is performed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **Archive Handling Libraries**  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Apache Commons Compress’s `TarArchiveInputStream`, `TarUtils`, and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveUtils` for how entry names are resolved and combined with output paths.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **FilePathTraversal Sanitizer**  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Hooks in `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal` to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand which file I/O calls are flagged and why.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Harness Entry Points**  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `[0m[1;35mTikaAppUntarringFuzzer.parseOne[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mfuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrace how the testcase is passed to Tika and ensure no additional transformations [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmask the vulnerability.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInvestigating these components will provide a holistic view of the path traversal [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue and where unsanitized entry names are accepted during tar extraction.[0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Summary of Root Cause  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The `TikaUntar` CLI tool resolves each TAR entry name via  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   but never verifies that the normalized `target` remains under `extractDir`. A [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious entry name like `..[0m[35m/[0m[95mevil.txt[0m[39m` will normalize to a parent directory, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing arbitrary writes outside the intended extraction folder. This triggers the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFilePathTraversal sanitizer.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Patch Steps  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.java`, locate the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile‐extraction loop around lines [0m[1;36m41[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m49[0m[39m.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Immediately after computing and normalizing the `target` path, insert a guard[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto verify the target is within the extraction directory.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. On violation, throw an `IOException` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe method already declares `throws [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, halting extraction and preventing traversal.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Leave all subsequent logic—directory creation and byte writing—unchanged so [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat safe archives continue to extract normally.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Implementation Plan  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Open `TikaUntar.java` and modify lines as follows:[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```diff[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m44[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m45[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m47[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are required to import statements beyond what's already present. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` is on the `main` signature, so no additional throws declarations are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneeded.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Unit Tests**: The existing `TikaUntarTest` uses well-formed entries under a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubfolder [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `test-documents/[0m[33m...[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. These will normalize to within `extractDir`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand pass the new prefix check, so tests remain green.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Archive APIs**: We do not alter how entries are read or how IO streams are [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanaged—only enforce a path‐prefix guard.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Harness & Fuzzer**: No harness or fuzzer code is modified; the build [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpipeline and fuzzing entry points remain unchanged.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & Safety  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Completeness**: A simple `startsWith` check on normalized paths is a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwell-established anti-traversal pattern.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimalism**: The patch is localized—no new utility methods, no sweeping [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges to dependencies or IO libraries.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Consistency**: Using `IOException` aligns with the method signature and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror model.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Test Compatibility**: As shown in existing tests, legitimate entries remain [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munaffected.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Performance Impact**: A single path comparison per file entry is negligible [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelative to extraction overhead.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Absolute Entry Names**: An absolute entry path will cause `[0m[1;35mresolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdiscard `extractDir` and produce a standalone absolute path. The prefix check will [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfail, preventing unexpected absolute writes.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Symlinks in Tar**: If symlink entries are later processed as files, they too[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill be guarded. Directories and other non-file entries are unaffected by this [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile‐only check.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Nested Symlinks**: If an extracted directory contains symlinks leading [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutside, that is outside this patch’s scope. Handling symlink resolution [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecursively would require deeper logic, which can be added in future iterations if [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneeded.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Next Steps  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Apply the above diff to the main codebase.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaUntarTest`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to confirm no regressions.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun fuzzing with Jazzer instrumentation to verify the FilePathTraversal [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue is resolved and no new sanitizer alerts are triggered.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis targeted fix enforces a proven canonicalization check, prevents the reported [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal vulnerability, and retains all existing functionality and tests.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue arises when the Jazzer fuzzing harness for Tika’s untar CLI [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`TikaUntar`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detects and reports a critical file path traversal vulnerability. The[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer run ends with a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception triggered by the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal` sanitizer.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA patch was proposed in `TikaUntar.java` to validate each archive entry’s [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction path. It adds a check that throws an `IOException` if the normalized [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget path does not start with the intended extraction directory.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen the patched code is re-fuzzed, the execution still terminates with a non-zero [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexit status. This time the crash is a `java.lang.RuntimeException: something went [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvery, very wrong` in the harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, caused by the newly [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduced `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Entry is outside the target dir: ..."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. The patch thus [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreplaces the sanitizer-triggered crash with an explicit exception in the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication code, but the harness still treats this as a crash.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause & Symptom Analysis[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness flags directory-traversal entries via the FilePathTraversal[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer. Our previous patch in `TikaUntar.main` prevented the sanitizer violation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby throwing an `IOException` for invalid entries, but this simply shifts the crash [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the sanitizer to the application. The harness treats any uncaught exception [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout of `main` as a crash, so the fuzz run still fails [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit status [0m[1;36m77[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must prevent directory‐escaping entries from being written, but do so [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout letting an exception propagate out of `main`. Instead, we should skip any [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry whose normalized path does not start with the intended extraction directory, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand continue processing the rest of the archive. This satisfies security [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while allowing `main` to complete normally [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Strategy[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Modify `tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.java` inside the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction loop:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Replace the `throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` guard with a simple `continue` to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskip the malicious entry.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Emit a warning or log message to STDERR or use the existing Tika[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogger to record that an entry was skipped. This does not affect exit status or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure that only entries whose normalized extraction path is a descendant of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe target directory are processed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirectories created and file written[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and all [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mothers are ignored.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do **not** wrap the entire `main` in a broad try-catch that hides genuine IO [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors. Only skip entries that fail the path check; allow real filesystem or I/O [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., permission issues[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to still propagate.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid archives: All file entries with safe paths continue to be extracted [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly as before [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent directories created, file content written[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TikaUntarTest`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: They rely on correct extraction of valid [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries; skipping only affects malicious entries that tests don’t include. No [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting behavior for well-formed inputs is changed.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to harness or test code: Fuzzer logic remains untouched; tests [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill pass; harness sees exit code [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m on invalid entries, so the fuzz run completes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout crashing on traversal.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Steps to Implement[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `TikaUntar.java` and locate the loop starting at line ~[0m[1;36m41[0m[39m:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtae != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.isFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              Path target = [0m[1;35mextractDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Immediately after normalizing `target`, insert the path‐check guard:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mextractDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Skip any entry outside of the extraction directory[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Optional: log warning[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  tae = [0m[1;35mtais.getNextEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  continue;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Remove the previous `throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` code block entirely.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the existing directory‐creation and write logic intact:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mFiles.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget, [0m[1;35mtais.readAllBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Ensure the `tae = [0m[1;35mtais.getNextEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` call stays at the end of the loop so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miteration continues normally.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & Side‐Effects[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By converting an exception‐based guard into a skip, we maintain the security [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno directory&nbsp;traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without producing a process‐terminating [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception. The fuzzer harness sees no uncaught exception, so the fuzzing run is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a “handled” case rather than a crash.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Normal I/O errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., disk full, permission issues[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m still throw [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` out of `main` and are correctly reported as failures. We are only [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintercepting and swallowing the specific logic‐error of path traversal.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests for valid extraction remain unaffected, as no valid entry will trigger [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe skip. Malicious or malformed entries are simply ignored.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications are required in any external or harness code, respecting the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrule that fuzzing logic/harness/test code must remain untouched.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References to Similar Code Paths[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Many archives‐handling tools [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., the Apache Commons utility `ArchiveUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskip or abort on invalid entries without raising an uncaught exception. Our [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproach follows that convention: detect → skip.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The same pattern is found in ZIP‐extraction code elsewhere in Tika, which [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moften ignores entries outside of a safe prefix.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mvn test`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure no regressions.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re‐fuzz with `TikaAppUntarringFuzzer`; confirm that:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No sanitizer violation is reported.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No unhandled exception propagates out of `main`.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Harness returns exit code [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m with an empty crash count.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally check logs to see “Skipping entry…” warnings when a [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal‐attempt input is fed.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>tika-app/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/cli/TikaUntar.jav[0m[1;92ma:39[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m53[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_r[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95mange[0m[39m>[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
